<h1 class="header"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Jurassic World</span>
            <span class="nobr">(<a href="/year/2015/?ref_=tt_ov_inf"
>2015</a>)</span>

</h1>
    <div class="infobar">



        



<a href="/genre/Action?ref_=tt_ov_inf"
><span class="itemprop" itemprop="genre">Action</span></a>
 <span class="ghost">|</span> 
<a href="/genre/Adventure?ref_=tt_ov_inf"
><span class="itemprop" itemprop="genre">Adventure</span></a>
 <span class="ghost">|</span> 
<a href="/genre/Sci-Fi?ref_=tt_ov_inf"
><span class="itemprop" itemprop="genre">Sci-Fi</span></a>
                &nbsp;-&nbsp;
            <span class="nobr">
<a href="/title/tt0369610/releaseinfo?ref_=tt_ov_inf+"
title="See all release dates" > 11 June 2015<meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-06-11" />
(Germany)
</a>            </span>

    </div>
 
<div class="star-box giga-star">
    <div class="star-box-rating-widget">

    </div> 
    <div class="clear"></div>

                        <p></p>
<p itemprop="description">
Twenty-two years after the events of <a href="/title/tt0107290">Jurassic Park</a> (1993), Isla Nublar now features a fully functioning dinosaur theme park, Jurassic World, as originally envisioned by John Hammond. After 10 years of operation and visitor rates declining, in order to fulfill a corporate mandate, a new attraction is created to re-spark visitor's interest, which backfires horribly.</p>
                        <p></p>
    <div class="txt-block" itemprop="director" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <h2>Storyline</h2>
        
        <div class="inline canwrap" itemprop="description">
            <p>
Twenty-two years after the events of <a href="/title/tt0107290?ref_=tt_stry_pl">Jurassic Park</a> (1993), Isla Nublar now features a fully functioning dinosaur theme park, Jurassic World, as originally envisioned by John Hammond. After 10 years of operation and visitor rates declining, in order to fulfill a corporate mandate, a new attraction is created to re-spark visitor's interest, which backfires horribly.            </p>
        </div>
        
        <span class="see-more inline"> 
                <a href="/title/tt0369610/plotsummary?ref_=tt_stry_pl"
>Plot Summary</a>
    <span>|</span>

>Add Synopsis</a>
    </span>

    <div id="titleDidYouKnow" class="article">
    <span class=rightcornerlink >
            <a href="/register/login?why=edit&ref_=tt_trv_trv"
rel="login">Edit</a>
    </span>
        <h2>Did You Know?</h2>
    <div id="trivia" class="txt-block">
        <h4>Trivia</h4>


When "Jurassic Park 4" was still in development, <a href="/name/nm0000368?ref_=tt_trv_trv">Laura Dern</a> was attached since 2007, as the only confirmed cast member, and stayed so until the plans were scrapped. With two appearances within four films, she is the most ubiquitous actress of the franchise. Of <a href="/title/tt0369610?ref_=tt_trv_trv">Jurassic World</a> (2015) she has said that she is "curious and excited" about the film, but jokes that she's relieved to not be a part of it: "I'm thrilled not to be chased by dinosaurs in this movie. I am tired".        <a href="trivia?ref_=tt_trv_trv"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>
                <hr />

            var url_sis3 = 'http://s.amazon-adsystem.com/iu3?',
                params_sis3 = [
                    "d=imdb.com",
                    "a1=",
                    "a2=01016d47a4666e5ec8ba82fc68e22fe0617fb345bcd7ad74829546acdd26fe23f667",
                    "pId=tt0369610",
                    "r=1",
                    "rP=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.imdb.com%2Ftitle%2Ftt0369610%2F",
                    "ex-hargs=v=1.0;c=IMDB;p=tt0369610;t=imdb_title_view;",
                    "encoding=server",
                    "cb=065842005232"  
                ];
        
            if (document.getElementById('sis_pixel_sitewide')) {
                (document.getElementById('sis_pixel_sitewide')).src = url_sis3 + params_sis3.join('&');
            }
        }
        catch(e){
            if ('consoleLog' in window){
                consoleLog('Pixel failure ' + e.toString(),'sis');
            }
            if (window.ueLogError) { 
                window.ueLogError(e);
            }
        }
    }, 20);
</script>
<!-- End SIS code -->
